Analysis of the Results
The new results show significant improvement in terms of validation loss. Let's analyze the key points:

Validation Loss Improvement:

The validation loss decreased to 1.8031596088409423 by the end of epoch 10, which is a significant improvement compared to the previous results.
The best validation loss recorded is 1.78654, indicating a model that is learning well and generalizing better on the validation data.
Stable GPU Utilization:

The GPU memory usage is stable, with an allocation of 2.1 GB and reservation of 3.5 GB throughout the training, which is within acceptable limits and indicates efficient memory management.
Training Progress:

The training progressed smoothly through 10 epochs and 5 folds of cross-validation, showing consistent improvement in validation loss.
The use of early stopping ensured that the best-performing model was saved.
Interpretation
Better Performance: The reduction in validation loss from previous runs to 1.8031596088409423 indicates that the model's performance has improved significantly. Lower validation loss generally means better generalization to unseen data.
Training Configuration: The adjustments made, such as reduced learning rate, increased epochs, and appropriate batch size, contributed to this improvement.
Recommendations
Further Tuning:

Continue fine-tuning hyperparameters such as learning rate, batch size, and number of epochs to explore if further improvements can be achieved.
Consider experimenting with different pre-trained models (e.g., roberta-base, distilbert-base-uncased) to compare performance.
Larger Dataset:

If possible, train the model on a larger dataset. More data generally helps the model learn better representations and generalize well.
Additional Techniques:

Implement techniques like data augmentation, dropout regularization, and advanced optimization algorithms to further improve model performance.
Evaluation Metrics:

Use additional evaluation metrics such as accuracy, precision, recall, and F1-score to get a more comprehensive understanding of model performance.
Conclusion
The current results show a marked improvement over previous attempts, indicating that the changes made have positively impacted the model's performance. Continued experimentation and tuning can potentially yield even better results.
